indexmap::IndexMap;\nuse serde::Deserialize;\n\nuse crate::error::{JigError, StructuredError};\n\n// ── Public types ────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub struct Recipe {\n    pub name: Option<String>,\n    pub description: Option<String>,\n    pub variables: IndexMap<String, VariableDecl>,\n    pub files: Vec<FileOp>,\n    /// Directory containing the recipe file (used for template resolution).\n    pub recipe_dir: PathBuf,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, serde::Serialize, Deserialize)]\n#[serde(rename_all = \"lowercase\")]\npub enum VarType {\n    String,\n    Number,\n    Boolean,\n    Array,\n    Object,\n    Enum,\n}\n\nimpl std::fmt::Display for VarType {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {\n        match self {\n            VarType::String => write!(f, \"string\"),\n            VarType::Number => write!(f, \"number\"),\n            VarType::Boolean => write!(f, \"boolean\"),\n            VarType::Array => write!(f, \"array\"),\n            VarType::Object => write!(f, \"object\"),\n            VarType::Enum => write!(f, \"enum\"),\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, serde::Serialize, Deserialize)]\npub struct VariableDecl {\n    #[serde(rename = \"type\")]\n    pub var_type: VarType,\n    #[serde(default)]\n    pub required: bool,\n    #[serde(default)]\n    pub default: Option<serde_json::Value>,\n    #[serde(default)]\n    pub description: Option<String>,\n    /// For enum type: allowed values.\n    #[serde(default)]\n    pub values: Option<Vec<String>>,\n    /// For array type: element type.\n    #[serde(default)]\n    pub items: Option<VarType>,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq)]\npub enum MatchPosition {\n    First,\n    Last,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub enum InjectMode {\n    After { pattern: String, at: MatchPosition },\n    Before { pattern: String, at: MatchPosition },\n    Prepend,\n    Append,\n}\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone)]\npub enum FileOp {\n    Create {\n        template: String,\n        to: String,\n        skip_if_exists: bool,\n    },\n    Inject {\n        template: String,\n        inject: String,\n        mode: InjectMode,\n        skip_if: Option<String>,\n    },\n}\n\nimpl FileOp {\n    pub fn op_type_str(&self) -> &'static str {\n        match self {\n            FileOp::Create { .. } => \"create\",\n            FileOp::Inject { .. } => \"inject\",\n        }\n    }\n\n    pub fn template(&self) -> &str {\n        match self {\n            FileOp::Create { template, .. } | FileOp::Inject { template, .. } => template,\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// ── Raw YAML deserialization (intermediate) ─────────────────────────\n\n#[derive(Deserialize)]\nstruct RawRecipe {\n    name: Option<String>,\n    description: Option<String>,\n    #[serde(default)]\n    variables: IndexMap<String, VariableDecl>,\n    #[serde(default)]\n    files: Vec<RawFileOp>,\n}\n\n#[derive(Deserialize)]\nstruct RawFileOp {\n    template: Option<String>,\n    to: Option<String>,\n    inject: Option<String>,\n    replace: Option<serde_yaml::Value>,\n    patch: Option<serde_yaml::Value>,\n    #[serde(default)]\n    skip_if_exists: bool,\n    after: Option<String>,\n    before: Option<String>,\n    #[serde(default)]\n    prepend: bool,\n    #[serde(default)]\n    append: bool,\n    #[serde(default)]\n    at: Option<String>,\n    skip_if: Option<String>,\n}\n\n// ── Parsing + validation ────────────────────────────────────────────\n\nimpl Recipe {\n    /// Load and validate a recipe from a YAML file.\n    pub fn load(path: &Path) -> Result<Self, JigError> {\n        let path = path\n            .canonicalize()\n            .map_err(|_| recipe_err(\n                \"recipe file not found\",\n                &path.display().to_string(),\n                \"the file does not exist at the specified path\",\n                \"check the file path and try again\",\n            ))?;\n\n        let content = std::fs::read_to_string(&path)\n            .map_err(|e| recipe_err(\n                \"cannot read recipe file\",\n                &path.display().to_string(),\n                &e.to_string(),\n                \"check file permissions\",\n            ))?;\n\n        let recipe_dir = path.parent().unwrap_or(Path::new(\".\")).to_path_buf();\n        Self::parse(&content, recipe_dir, &path)\n    }\n\n    /// Parse recipe YAML content with a known recipe directory and source path.\n    pub fn parse(yaml: &str, recipe_dir: PathBuf, source_path: &Path) -> Result<Self, JigError> {\n        let raw: RawRecipe = serde_yaml::from_str(yaml)\n            .map_err(|e| recipe_err(\n                \"malformed recipe YAML\",\n                &source_path.display().to_string(),\n                &e.to_string(),\n                \"check YAML syntax — ensure proper indentation and field names\",\n            ))?;\n\n        let mut files = Vec::with_capacity(raw.files.len());\n        for (i, raw_op) in raw.files.into_iter().enumerate() {\n            let op = convert_file_op(raw_op, i, source_path)?;\n            files.push(op);\n        }\n\n        let recipe = Recipe {\n            name: raw.name,\n            description: raw.description,\n            variables: raw.variables,\n            files,\n            recipe_dir: recipe_dir.clone(),\n        };\n\n        // Validate template files exist.\n        recipe.validate_templates()?;\n\n        Ok(recipe)\n    }\n\n    fn validate_templates(&self) -> Result<(), JigError> {\n        for (i, op) in self.files.iter().enumerate() {\n            let tmpl = op.template();\n            let resolved = self.recipe_dir.join(tmpl);\n            if !resolved.is_file() {\n                return Err(recipe_err(\n                    &format!(\"template file not found: '{tmpl}'\"),\n                    &format!(\"files[{i}].template in recipe\"),\n                    &format!(\"looked for '{}' but it does not exist\", resolved.display()),\n                    \"ensure the template file exists relative to the recipe file location\",\n                ));\n            }\n        }\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Resolve a template path relative to the recipe directory.\n    #[allow(dead_code)] // Used in later phases\n    pub fn resolve_template(&self, template: &str) -> PathBuf {\n        self.recipe_dir.join(template)\n    }\n}\n\n/// Convert a raw file op into a typed FileOp, validating structure.\nfn convert_file_op(raw: RawFileOp, index: usize, source: &Path) -> Result<FileOp, JigError> {\n    let loc = format!(\"files[{index}] in {}\", source.display());\n\n    // Template is required for all operations.\n    let template = raw.template.ok_or_else(|| recipe_err(\n        \"missing required field 'template'\",\n        &loc,\n        \"every file operation must specify a template\",\n        \"add a 'template' field pointing to the Jinja2 template file\",\n    ))?;\n\n    // Count how many operation-type fields are present.\n    let has_to = raw.to.is_some();\n    let has_inject = raw.inject.is_some();\n    let has_replace = raw.replace.is_some();\n    let has_patch = raw.patch.is_some();\n    let type_count = [has_to, has_inject, has_replace, has_patch]\n        .iter()\n        .filter(|&&b| b)\n        .count();\n\n    if type_count == 0 {\n        return Err(recipe_err(\n            \"missing operation type\",\n            &loc,\n            \"file operation must specify one of: 'to' (create), 'inject', 'replace', or 'patch'\",\n            \"add a 'to' field for create or an 'inject' field for injection\",\n        ));\n    }\n    if type_count > 1 {\n        let mut present = Vec::new();\n        if has_to { present.push(\"to\"); }\n        if has_inject { present.push(\"inject\"); }\n        if has_replace { present.push(\"replace\"); }\n        if has_patch { present.push(\"patch\"); }\n        return Err(recipe_err(\n            &format!(\"ambiguous operation type: found multiple of {}\", present.join(\", \")),\n            &loc,\n            \"a file operation must specify exactly one operation type\",\n            \"remove extra fields so only one of 'to', 'inject', 'replace', or 'patch' remains\",\n        ));\n    }\n\n    // Reject unsupported operation types (v0.1).\n    if has_replace {\n        return Err(recipe_err(\n            \"unknown operation type 'replace'            to: raw.to.unwrap(),\n            skip_if_exists: raw.skip_if_exists,\n        })\n    } else {\n        // has_inject\n        let inject_target = raw.inject.unwrap();\n        let mode = parse_inject_mode(&raw.after, &raw.before, raw.prepend, raw.append, &raw.at, index, source)?;\n        Ok(FileOp::Inject {\n            template,\n            inject: inject_target,\n            mode,\n            skip_if: raw.skip_if,\n        })\n    }\n}\n\n/// Parse and validate injection mode from raw fields.\nfn parse_inject_mode(\n    after: &Option<String>,\n    before: &Option<String>,\n    prepend: bool,\n    append: bool,\n    at: &Option<String>,\n    index: usize,\n    source: &Path,\n) -> Result<InjectMode, JigError> {\n    let loc = format!(\"files[{index}] in return Err(recipe_err(\n            \"inject operation missing mode\",\n            &loc,\n            \"inject must specify one of: 'after', 'before', 'prepend: true', or 'append: true'\",\n            \"add an injection mode field\",\n        ));\n    }\n    if mode_count > 1 {\n        return Err(recipe_err(\n            \"inject operation has conflicting modes\",\n            &loc,\n            \"only one of 'after', 'before', 'prepend', 'append' may be specified\",\n            \"remove extra injection mode fields so only one remains\",\n        ));\n    }\n\n    let pos = parse_match_position(at, index, source)?;\n\n    if let Some(pattern) = after {\n        validate_regex(pattern, \"after\", index, source)?;\n        Ok(InjectMode::After { pattern: pattern.clone(), at: pos })\n    } else if let Some(pattern) = before {\n        validate_regex(pattern, \"before\", index, source)?;\n        Ok(InjectMode::Before { pattern: pattern.clone(), at: pos })\n    } else VarType::Boolean => item.is_boolean(),\n            VarType::Array => item.is_array(),\n            VarType::Object => item.is_object(),\n            VarType::Enum => item.is_string(), // enum items err: &minijinja::Error,\n    source_path: &str,\n    template_source: &str,\n    vars: &Value,\n) -> JigError {\n    let kind = err.kind();\n    let line_info = err.line().map(|l| format!(\" (line {})\", l)).unwrap_or_default();\n\n    match kind {\n        minijinja::ErrorKind::UndefinedError => {\n            // minijinja doesn't include the variable name in the error.\n            // Extract &minijinja::Error) -> JigError {\n    let line_info = err.line().map(|l| format!(\" (line {})\", l)).unwrap_or_default();\n    let detail = err.detail().unwrap_or(\"syntax error\");\n\n    JigError::TemplateRendering(StructuredError {\n        what: \"template syntax error\".into(),\n        where_: format!(\"{}{}\", template_name, line_info),\n        why: detail.to_string(),\n        hint: \"check Jinja2 syntax — ensure all blocks are properly closed\".into(),\n    })\n}\n\n/// Find the undefined variable in a template by scanning for references\n/// not present in the variable context.\nfn find_undefined_variable(template_source: &str, error_line: Option<usize>, vars: &Value) -> String {\n    let var_keys: Vec<&str> = match vars.as_object() {\n        Some(obj) => obj.keys().map(|s| s.as_str()).collect(),\n        None => vec![],\n    };\n\n    // Extract variable references from the template.\n    // Matches {{ name }}, {{ name | filter }}, {{ name.attr }}, etc.\n    let re = regex::Regex::new(r\"\\{\\{[\\s-]*([a-zA-Z_][a-zA-Z0-9_]*)\").unwrap();\n    // Also check {% if/for/elif blocks\n    let block_re = regex::Regex::new(r\"\\{%[\\s-]*(?:if|elif|for\\s+\\w+\\s+in|set\\s+\\w+\\s*=)\\s+([a-zA-Z_][a-zA-Z0-9_]*)\").unwrap();\n\n    let lines: Vec<&str> = template_source.lines().collect();\n\n    // If we have a line number, check that line first\n    if let Some(line_num) = error_line.filter(|&l| l > 0 && l <= lines.len()) {\n        let line = lines[line_num - 1];\n        for cap in re.captures_iter(line).chain(block_re.captures_iter(line)) {\n            let name = &cap[1];\n            if !var_keys.contains(&name) {\n                return name.to_string();\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Fall back to scanning the entire template\n    for cap in re.captures_iter(template_source).chain(block_re.captures_iter(template_source)) {\n        let name = &cap[1];\n        if !var_keys.contains(&name) {\n            return name.to_string();\n        }\n    }\n\n    \"unknown\".to_string()\n}\n\n/// Generate a \"did you mean?\" hint using Levenshtein distance.\n/// Looks at all keys in the provided variable context.\nfn did_you_mean_hint(var_name: &str, vars: &Value) -> String {\n    let keys: Vec<&str> = match vars.as_object() {\n        Some(obj) => obj.keys().map(|s| s.as_str()).collect(),\n        None => return format!(\"check variable name '{var_name}'\"),\n    };\n\n    if keys.is_empty() {\n        return format!(\"check variable name '{}' — no variables were provided\", var_name);\n    }\n\n    let mut best_match: Option<(&str, usize)> = None;\n    for key in &keys {\n        let dist = strsim::levenshtein(var_name, key);\n        if dist <= 3 && (best_match.is_none() || dist < best_match.unwrap().1) {\n            best_match = Some((key, dist));\n        }\n    }\n\n    match best_match {\n        Some((suggestion, _)) => format!(\"did you mean '{suggestion}'?\"),\n        None => format!(\"check variable name '{}' — available variables: {}\", var_name, keys.join(\", \")),\n    }\n}\n\n// ── Tests inject;\n\nuse std::collections::HashMap;\nuse std::path::{Path, PathBuf};\n\nuse crate::error::{JigError, StructuredError};\nuse crate::recipe::FileOp;\n\n// ── Execution context ─────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// Shared state for operation execution.\npub struct ExecutionContext {\n    /// Base directory for resolving output paths (default: cwd).\n    pub base_dir: PathBuf,\n    /// If true, produce output but write nothing to disk.\n    pub dry_run: bool,\n    /// If true, overwrite existing files on create.\n    pub force: bool,\n    /// Virtual file state for dry-run mode: path -> content.\n    /// Create ops populate this instead of writing to disk.\n    /// Inject ops read from here if the target was created in the same run.\n    pub virtual_files: HashMap<PathBuf, String>,\n}\n\nimpl ExecutionContext {\n    pub fn new(base_dir: PathBuf, dry_run: bool, force: bool) -> Self {\n        Self {\n            base_dir,\n            dry_run,\n            force,\n            virtual_files: HashMap::new(),\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Resolve an output path relative to the base directory.\n    pub fn resolve_path(&self, relative: &str) -> PathBuf {\n        self.base_dir.join(relative)\n    }\n}\n\n// ── Operation result ──────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// Result of a single file operation.\n#[derive(Debug)]\npub enum OpResult {\n    Success {\n        action: &'static str,\n        path: PathBuf,\n        lines: usize,\n        location: Option<String>,\n        rendered_content: Option<String>,\n    },\n    Skip {\n        path: PathBuf,\n        reason: String,\n        rendered_content: Option<String>,\n    },\n    Error {\n        path: PathBuf,\n        error: StructuredError,\n        rendered_content: String,\n    },\n}\n\nimpl OpResult {\n    pub fn path(&self) -> &Path {\n        match self {\n            OpResult::Success { path, .. }\n            | OpResult::Skip { path, .. }\n            | OpResult::Error { path, .. } => path,\n        }\n    }\n\n    pub fn is_error(&self) -> bool {\n        matches!(self, OpResult::Error { .. })\n    }\n\n    pub fn is_write(&self) -> bool {\n        matches!(self, OpResult::Success { .. })\n    }\n}\n\n// ── Dispatch ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// Pre-rendered operation ready for execution.\npub struct PreparedOp {\n    pub file_op: FileOp,\n    pub rendered_content: String,\n    pub rendered_path: String,\n    /// For inject: rendered skip_if string (if any).\n    pub rendered_skip_if: Option<String>,\n}\n\n/// Execute a single prepared operation.\npub fn execute_operation(\n    prepared: &PreparedOp,\n    ctx: &mut ExecutionContext,\n    verbose: bool,\n) -> OpResult {\n    match &prepared.file_op {\n        FileOp::Create { skip_if_exists, .. } => {\n            create::execute(\n                &prepared.rendered_path,\n                &prepared.rendered_content,\n                *skip_if_exists,\n                ctx,\n                verbose,\n            )\n        }\n        FileOp::Inject { mode, .. } => {\n            inject::execute(\n                &prepared.rendered_path,\n                &prepared.rendered_content,\n                prepared.rendered_skip_if.as_deref(),\n                mode,\n                ctx,\n                verbose,\n            )\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Convert an OpResult::Error into a JigError for fail-fast propagation.\npub fn op_error_to_jig_error(result: &OpResult) -> Option<JigError> {\n    match result {\n        OpResult::Error { error, .. } => Some(JigError::FileOperation(error.clone())),\n        _ => None,\n    }\n}\n","exit_code":0,"status":"completed"}}

crate::error::StructuredError;\nuse crate::recipe::{InjectMode, MatchPosition};\n\nuse super::{ExecutionContext, OpResult};\n\n/// Execute an inject operation: insert rendered content into an existing file.\n///\n/// - `rendered_path` is the already-rendered target file path.\n/// - `rendered_content` is the template output to inject.\n/// - `rendered_skip_if` is the rendered skip_if string (if any).\n/// - `mode` determines where to inject (after/before regex, prepend, append).\n/// - Reads from virtual_files if target was created in same run, else from disk.\n/// - Updates virtual_files with post-injection content for subsequent operations.\npub fn execute(\n    rendered_path: &str,\n    rendered_content: &str,\n    rendered_skip_if: Option<&str>,\n    mode: &InjectMode,\n    ctx: &mut ExecutionContext,\n    verbose: bool,\n) -> OpResult {\n    let target = ctx.resolve_path(rendered_path);\n    let injected_lines = rendered_content.lines().count();\n    let content_for_verbose = if verbose {\n        Some(rendered_content.to_string())\n    } else {\n        None\n    };\n\n    // Read target file content: prefer virtual_files, then disk.\n    let file_content = if let Some(content) = ctx.virtual_files.get(&target) {\n        content.clone()\n    } else {\n        match std::fs::read_to_string(&target) {\n            Ok(content) => content,\n            Err(_) => {\n                return OpResult::Error {\n                    path: target.clone(),\n                    error: StructuredError {\n                        what: format!(\"target file not found: '{}'\", target.display()),\n                        where_: target.display().to_string(),\n                        why: \"the file does not exist and was not created by a prior operation in this run\".into(),\n                        hint: \"ensure the target file exists, or add a create operation before this inject\".into(),\n                    },\n                    rendered_content: rendered_content.to_string(),\n                };\n            }\n        }\n    };\n\n    // Check skip_if: if the rendered string is found in the file, skip.\n    if let Some(skip_str) = rendered_skip_if\n        && file_content.contains(skip_str)\n    {\n        return OpResult::Skip {\n            path: target,\n            reason: format!(\"skip_if matched: {skip_str}\"),\n            rendered_content: content_for_verbose,\n        };\n    }\n\n    // Perform injection based on mode.\n    let (new_content, location) = match mode {\n        InjectMode::After { pattern, at } => {\n            match inject_after_before(&file_content, rendered_content, pattern, at, true, &target) {\n                Ok(v) => v,\n                Err(op_result) => return op_result,\n            }\n        }\n        InjectMode::Before { pattern, at } => {\n            match inject_after_before(&file_content, rendered_content, pattern, at, false, &target) {\n                Ok(v) => v,\n                Err(op_result) => return op_result,\n            }\n        }\n        InjectMode::Prepend => {\n            let mut result = String::with_capacity(rendered_content.len() + file_content.len() + 1);\n            result.push_str(rendered_content);\n            if !rendered_content.ends_with('\\n') && !file_content.is_empty() {\n                result.push('\\n');\n            }\n            result.push_str(&file_content);\n            (result, \"prepend\".to_string())\n        }\n        InjectMode::Append => {\n            let mut result = String::with_capacity(file_content.len() + rendered_content.len() + 1);\n            result.push_str(&file_content);\n            if !file_content.ends_with('\\n') && !file_content.is_empty() {\n                result.push('\\n');\n            }\n            result.push_str(rendered_content);\n            (result, \"append\".to_string())\n        }\n    };\n\n    // Write the modified content.\n    if ctx.dry_run {\n        ctx.virtual_files.insert(target.clone(), new_content);\n    } else {\n        if let Err(e) = std::fs::write(&target, &new_content) {\n            return OpResult::Error {\n                path: target.clone(),\n                error: StructuredError {\n                    what: format!(\"cannot write file '{}'\", target.display()),\n                    where_: target.display().to_string(),\n                    why: e.to_string(),\n                    hint: \"check file permissions\".into(),\n                },\n                rendered_content: rendered_content.to_string(),\n            };\n        }\n        // Also update virtual_files so subsequent ops in this run see the new content.\n        ctx.virtual_files.insert(target.clone(), new_content);\n    }\n\n    OpResult::Success {\n        action: \"inject\",\n        path: target,\n        lines: injected_lines,\n        location: Some(location),\n        rendered_content: content_for_verbose,\n    }\n}\n\n/// Inject content after or before a regex match.\n/// Returns (new_content, location_description) or an OpResult::Error.\n#[allow(clippy::result_large_err)]\nfn inject_after_before(\n    file_content: &str,\n    rendered_content: &str,\n    pattern: &str,\n    at: &MatchPosition,\n    is_after: bool,\n    target: &std::path::Path,\n) -> Result<(String, String), OpResult> {\n    let re = Regex::new(pattern).expect(\"regex was validated at parse time\");\n\n    let lines: Vec<&str> = file_content.lines().collect();\n    let matching_indices: Vec<usize> = lines\n        .iter()\n        .enumerate()\n        .filter(|(_, line)| re.is_match(line))\n        .map(|(i, _)| i)\n        .collect();\n\n    if matching_indices.is_empty() {\n        return Err(OpResult::Error {\n            path: target.to_path_buf(),\n            error: StructuredError {\n                what: format!(\"regex pattern matched no lines in '{}'\", target.display()),\n                where_: target.display().to_string(),\n                why: format!(\"pattern '{}' did not match any line in the file\", pattern),\n                hint: \"check the regex pattern against the file contents\".into(),\n            },\n            rendered_content: rendered_content.to_string(),\n        });\n    }\n\n    let match_idx = match at {\n        MatchPosition::First => matching_indices[0],\n        MatchPosition::Last => *matching_indices.last().unwrap(),\n    };\n\n    // Build new content by inserting at the right position.\n    let direction = if is_after { \"after\" } else { \"before\" };\n    let at_str = match at {\n        MatchPosition::First => \"first\",\n        MatchPosition::Last => \"last\",\n    };\n    // Line numbers are 1-based for human display.\n    let location = format!(\"{direction}:{pattern} ({at_str} match, line {})\", match_idx + 1);\n\n    let mut result = String::new();\n    let has_trailing_newline = file_content.ends_with('\\n');\n\n    if is_after {\n        // Insert after match_idx line.\n        for (i, line) in lines.iter().enumerate() {\n            result.push_str(line);\n            result.push('\\n');\n            if i == match_idx {\n                result.push_str(rendered_content);\n                if !rendered_content.ends_with('\\n') {\n                    result.push('\\n');\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    } else {\n        // Insert before match_idx line.\n        for (i, line) in lines.iter().enumerate() {\n            if i == match_idx {\n                result.push_str(rendered_content);\n                if !rendered_content.ends_with('\\n') {\n                    result.push('\\n');\n                }\n            }\n            result.push_str(line);\n            result.push('\\n');\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Preserve original trailing newline behavior.\n    if !has_trailing_newline && result.ends_with('\\n') {\n        result.pop();\n    }\n\n    Ok((result, location))\n}\n\n// ── Tests ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n#[cfg(test)]\nmod tests {\n    use super::*;\n    use std::fs;\n    use tempfile::TempDir;\n\n    fn make_ctx(dir: &std::path::Path, dry_run: bool, force: bool) -> ExecutionContext {\n        ExecutionContext::new(dir.to_path_buf(), dry_run, force)\n    }\n\n    // ── AC-5.1: after inserts content on line after first match ──\n\n    #[test]\n    fn ac_5_1_after_first_match() {\n        let dir = TempDir::new().unwrap();\n    let mode = InjectMode::After {\n            pattern: \"^# fixtures\".into(),\n            at: MatchPosition::First,\n        };\n        let result = execute(\"target.py\", \"fixture_c = 3\\n\", None, &mode, &mut ctx, false);\n\n        assert!(matches!(&result, OpResult::Success { action: \"inject\", .. }));\n        let content = fs::read_to_string(&target).unwrap();\n        let lines: Vec<&str> = content.lines().collect();\n        assert_eq!(lines[0], \"# fixtures\");\n        assert_eq!(lines[1], \"fixture_c = 3\");\n        assert_eq!(lines[2], \"fixture_a = 1\");\n    }\n\n {"type":"item.completed","item":{"id":"item_21","type":"command_execution","command":"/bin/zsh -lc \"sed -n '1,420p' src/output.rs\"","aggregated_output":"use std::io::IsTerminal;\n\nuse indexmap::IndexSet;\nuse owo_colors::OwoColorize;\nuse serde_json::Value;\n\nuse crate::operations::OpResult;\n\n// ── Output mode ───────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq)]\npub enum OutputMode {\n    /// JSON to stdout (piped or --json).\n    Json,\n    /// Human-readable colored text to stderr.\n    Human,\n}\n\n/// Determine output mode from flags and TTY detection.\n/// --json forces JSON. Otherwise: piped → JSON, TTY → Human.\npub fn detect_mode(force_json: bool) -> OutputMode {\n    if force_json || !std::io::stdout().is_terminal() {\n        OutputMode::Json\n    } else {\n        OutputMode::Human\n    }\n}\n\n// ── JSON output ───────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// Build the full JSON output object for `jig run`.\npub fn format_json(results: &[OpResult], dry_run: bool, verbose: bool) -> Value {\n    let operations: Vec<Value> = results.iter().map(|r| op_result_to_json(r, verbose)).collect();\n    let (files_written, files_skipped) = compute_file_summaries(results);\n\n    serde_json::json!({\n        \"dry_run\": dry_run,\n        \"operations\": operations,\n        \"files_written\": files_written.into_iter().collect::<Vec<_>>(),\n        \"files_skipped\": files_skipped.into_iter().collect::<Vec<_>>(),\n    })\n}\n\nfn op_result_to_json(result: &OpResult, verbose: bool) -> Value {\n    match result {\n        OpResult::Success { action, path, lines, location, rendered_content } => {\n            let mut obj = serde_json::json!({\n                \"action\": action,\n                \"path\": path.display().to_string(),\n                \"lines\": lines,\n            });\n            if let Some(loc) = location {\n                obj[\"location\"] = Value::String(loc.clone());\n            }\n            if verbose\n                && let Some(content) = rendered_content {\n                    obj[\"rendered_content\"] = Value::String(content.clone());\n                }\n            obj\n        }\n        OpResult::Skip { path, reason, rendered_content } => {\n            let mut obj = serde_json::json!({\n                \"action\": \"skip\",\n                \"path\": path.display().to_string(),\n                \"reason\": reason,\n            });\n            if verbose\n                && let Some(content) = rendered_content {\n                    obj[\"rendered_content\"] = Value::String(content.clone());\n                }\n            obj\n        }\n        OpResult::Error { path, error, rendered_content } => {\n            serde_json::json!({\n                \"action\": \"error\",\n                \"path\": path.display().to_string(),\n                \"what\": error.what,\n                \"where\": error.where_,\n                \"why\": error.why,\n                \"hint\": error.hint,\n                \"rendered_content\": rendered_content,\n            })\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Compute files_written and files_skipped arrays.\n/// A path appears in files_written if any operation wrote to it.\n/// A path appears in files_skipped only if ALL operations targeting it were skipped.\n/// Paths appear in order of first encounter.\nfn compute_file_summaries(results: &[OpResult]) -> (IndexSet<String>, IndexSet<String>) {\n    let mut written: IndexSet<String> = IndexSet::new();\n    let mut skipped: IndexSet<String> = IndexSet::new();\n\n    for result in results {\n        let path_str = result.path().display().to_string();\n\n        match result {\n            OpResult::Success { .. } => {\n                written.insert(path_str.clone());\n                // If it was previously only in skipped, remove it.\n                skipped.swap_remove(&path_str);\n            }\n            OpResult::Skip { .. } => {\n                // Only add to skipped if not already written.\n                if !written.contains(&path_str) {\n                    skipped.insert(path_str);\n                }\n            }\n            OpResult::Error { .. } => {\n                // Errors don't affect file summaries (fail-fast means this is the last op).\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    (written, skipped)\n}\n\n// ── Human output ──────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// Write human-readable output to stderr.\npub fn format_human(results: &[OpResult], dry_run: bool, verbose: bool) {\n    if dry_run {\n        eprintln!(\"{}\", \"(dry run)\".dimmed());\n    }\n\n    for result in results {\n        match result {\n            OpResult::Success { action, path, lines, location, rendered_content } => {\n                let action_str = action.to_string();\n                eprint!(\"  {} {}\", action_str.green(), path.display());\n                if let Some(loc) = location {\n                    eprint!(\" ({})\", loc);\n                }\n                eprintln!(\" ({} lines)\", lines);\n                if verbose\n                    && let Some(content) = rendered_content {\n                        for line in content.lines() {\n                            eprintln!(\"    {}\", line.dimmed());\n                        }\n                    }\n            }\n            OpResult::Skip { path, reason, rendered_content } => {\n                eprintln!(\"  {} {} — {}\", \"skip\".yellow(), path.display(), reason);\n                if verbose\n                    && let Some(content) = rendered_content {\n                        for line in content.lines() {\n                            eprintln!(\"    {}\", line.dimmed());\n                        }\n                    }\n            }\n            OpResult::Error { path, error, rendered_content } => {\n                eprintln!(\"  {} {}\", \"error\".red(), path.display());\n                eprintln!(\"    what: {}\", error.what);\n                eprintln!(\"    where: {}\", error.where_);\n                eprintln!(\"    why: {}\", error.why);\n                eprintln!(\"    hint: {}\", error.hint);\n                if verbose || !rendered_content.is_empty() {\n                    eprintln!(\"    rendered content ({} lines):\", rendered_content.lines().count());\n                    for line in rendered_content.lines() {\n                        eprintln!(\"      {}\", line.dimmed());\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    let (written, skipped) = compute_file_summaries(results);\n    if !written.is_empty() || !skipped.is_empty() {\n        eprintln!();\n        if !written.is_empty() {\n            eprintln!(\n                \"{}: {}\",\n                if dry_run { \"would write\" } else { \"wrote\" },\n                written.len()\n            );\n        }\n        if !skipped.is_empty() {\n            eprintln!(\"skipped: {}\", skipped.len());\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// ── Tests Fixture-based integration tests for jig CLI.\n//!\n//! Each subdirectory under `tests/fixtures/` is a test case. Adding a new test\n//! case requires only adding a directory — no code changes.\n//!\n//! Fixture layout:\n//!   recipe.yaml          — recipe to run\n//!   vars.json            — variables (JSON)\n//!   templates/           — template files (referenced by recipe)\n//!   existing/            — pre-existing files, copied to temp dir before run\n//!   expected/            — expected files after run (diffed against actual)\n//!   expected_output.json — (optional) expected JSON output structure\n//!   expected_exit_code   — (optional) expected exit code (default: 0)\n//!   force                — (optional) if present, pass --force\n\nuse std::fs;\nuse std::path::{Path, PathBuf};\nuse std::process::Command;\n\n// ── Helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\nfn jig_bin() -> PathBuf {\n    PathBuf::from(env!(\"CARGO_BIN_EXE_jig\"))\n}\n\nfn fixtures_dir() -> PathBuf {\n    PathBuf::from(env!(\"CARGO_MANIFEST_DIR\")).join(\"tests/fixtures\")\n}\n\n/// Discover all fixture directories (immediate children of tests/fixtures/).\nfn discover_fixtures() -> Vec<PathBuf> {\n    let dir = fixtures_dir();\n    let mut fixtures: Vec<PathBuf> = fs::read_dir(&dir)\n        .unwrap_or_else(|e| panic!(\"cannot read fixtures dir {}: {}\", dir.display(), e))\n        .filter_map(|entry| {\n            let entry = entry.ok()?;\n            let path = entry.path();\n            if path.is_dir() && path.join(\"recipe.yaml\").exists() {\n                Some(path)\n            } else {\n                None\n            }\n        })\n        .collect();\n    fixtures.sort();\n    fixtures\n}\n\n/// Read expected exit code from fixture (default 0).\nfn expected_exit_code(fixture: &Path) -> i32 {\n    let path = fixture.join(\"expected_exit_code\");\n    if path.exists() {\n        fs::read_to_string(&path)\n            .unwrap()\n            .trim()\n            .parse()\n            .unwrap_or_else(|e| panic!(\"bad expected_exit_code in {}: {}\", fixture.display(), e))\n    } else {\n        0\n    }\n}\n\n/// Run jig on a fixture, returning (exit_code, stdout, stderr).\nfn run_fixture(fixture: &Path, work_dir: &Path) -> (i32, String, String) {\n    let recipe = fixture.join(\"recipe.yaml\");\n    let vars_json = fs::read_to_string(fixture.join(\"vars.json\")).unwrap_or_else(|_| \"{}\".into());\n\n    let mut cmd = Command::new(jig_bin());\n    cmd.args([\"run\", &recipe.display().to_string()])\n        .args([\"--vars\", &vars_json])\n        .args([\"--base-dir\", &work_dir.display().to_string()])\n        .arg(\"--json\");\n\n    if fixture.join(\"force\").exists() {\n        cmd.arg(\"--force\");\n    }\n\n    let output = cmd.output().expect(\"failed to run jig\");\n\n    let code = output.status.code().unwrap_or(-1);\n    let stdout = String::from_utf8_lossy(&output.stdout).to_string();\n    let stderr = String::from_utf8_lossy(&output.stderr).to_string();\n    (code, stdout, stderr)\n}\n\n/// Copy existing/ files into work_dir.\nfn setup_existing(fixture: &Path, work_dir: &Path) {\n    let existing = fixture.join(\"existing\");\n    if existing.is_dir() {\n        copy_dir_recursive(&existing, work_dir);\n    }\n}\n\n/// Recursively copy src/ contents into dst/.\nfn copy_dir_recursive(src: &Path, dst: &Path) {\n    for entry in fs::read_dir(src).unwrap() {\n        let entry = entry.unwrap();\n        let src_path = entry.path();\n        let dst_path = dst.join(entry.file_name());\n        if src_path.is_dir() {\n            fs::create_dir_all(&dst_path).unwrap();\n            copy_dir_recursive(&src_path, &dst_path);\n        } else {\n            if let Some(parent) = dst_path.parent() {\n                fs::create_dir_all(parent).unwrap();\n            }\n            fs::copy(&src_path, &dst_path).unwrap();\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Compare work_dir contents against expected/ directory.\n/// Returns a list of (relative_path, diff_description) for mismatches.\nfn diff_expected(fixture: &Path, work_dir: &Path) -> Vec<(String, String)> {\n    let expected = fixture.join(\"expected\");\n    if !expected.is_dir() {\n        return vec![];\n    }\n\n    let mut diffs = vec![];\n    diff_dir_recursive(&expected, work_dir, &expected, &mut diffs);\n    diffs\n}\n\nfn diff_dir_recursive(\n    expected_root: &Path,\n    work_dir: &Path,\n    current: &Path,\n    diffs: &mut Vec<(String, String)>,\n) {\n    for entry in fs::read_dir(current).unwrap() {\n        let entry = entry.unwrap();\n        let path = entry.path();\n        let rel = path.strip_prefix(expected_root).unwrap();\n\n        if path.is_dir() {\n            diff_dir_recursive(expected_root, work_dir, &path, diffs);\n        } else {\n            let actual_path = work_dir.join(rel);\n            if !actual_path.exists() {\n                diffs.push((rel.display().to_string(), \"file missing\".into()));\n                continue;\n            }\n            let expected_bytes = fs::read(&path).unwrap();\n            let actual_bytes = fs::read(&actual_path).unwrap();\n            if expected_bytes != actual_bytes {\n                let expected_str = String::from_utf8_lossy(&expected_bytes);\n                let actual_str = String::from_utf8_lossy(&actual_bytes);\n                diffs.push((\n                    rel.display().to_string(),\n                    format!(\n                        \"content mismatch:\\n--- expected\\n+++ actual\\n-{}\\n+{}\",\n                        expected_str.replace('\\n', \"\\n-\"),\n                        actual_str.replace('\\n', \"\\n+\"),\n                    ),\n                ));\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/// Normalize JSON output: replace absolute paths with relative paths\n/// (strip the work_dir prefix).\nfn normalize_json(json_str: &str, work_dir: &Path) -> serde_json::Value {\n    let work_dir_str = work_dir.display().to_string();\n    let normalized = json_str.replace(&format!(\"{}/\", work_dir_str), \"\");\n    serde_json::from_str(&normalized).unwrap_or_else(|e| {\n        panic!(\"failed to parse JSON output: {}\\nraw output:\\n{}\", e, json_str)\n    })\n}\n\n/// Assert JSON output matches expected_output.json.\n/// Only checks fields present in expected — extra fields in actual are allowed.\nfn assert_json_matches(expected: &serde_json::Value, actual: &serde_json::Value, path: &str) {\n    match (expected, actual) {\n        (serde_json::Value::Object(exp_map), serde_json::Value::Object(act_map)) => {\n            for (key, exp_val) in exp_map {\n                let act_val = act_map.get(key).unwrap_or_else(|| {\n                    panic!(\"missing key '{}' at {}\\nactual: {}\", key, path, actual)\n                });\n                assert_json_matches(exp_val, act_val, &format!(\"{}.{}\", path, key));\n            }\n        }\n        (serde_json::Value::Array(exp_arr), serde_json::Value::Array(act_arr)) => {\n            assert_eq!(\n                exp_arr.len(),\n                act_arr.len(),\n                \"array length mismatch at {}\\nexpected: {}\\nactual: {}\",\n                path,\n                expected,\n                actual\n            );\n            for (i, (exp, act)) in exp_arr.iter().zip(act_arr.iter()).enumerate() {\n                assert_json_matches(exp, act, &format!(\"{}[{}]\", path, i));\n            }\n        }\n        _ => {\n            assert_eq!(\n                expected, actual,\n                \"value mismatch at {}\\nexpected: {}\\nactual: {}\",\n                path, expected, actual\n            );\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// ── Core test runner ─────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// Run a single fixture test case.\nfn run_fixture_test(fixture: &Path) {\n    let name = fixture.file_name().unwrap().to_str().unwrap();\n    let tmp = tempfile::TempDir::new().unwrap();\n    let work_dir = tmp.path();\n\n    // expected_code = expected_exit_code(fixture);\n    assert_eq!(\n        exit_code, expected_code,\n        \"fixture '{}': expected exit code {}, got {}\\nstdout: {}\\nstderr: {}\",\n        name, expected_code, exit_code, stdout, stderr\n    );\n\n    // For success cases, diff expected files.\n    if expected_code == 0 {\n        let diffs = diff_expected(fixture, work_dir);\n        assert!(\n            diffs.is_empty(),\n            \"fixture '{}': file mismatches:\\n{}\",\n            name,\n            diffs\n                .iter()\n                .map(|(p, d)| format!(\"  {}: {}\", p, d))\n                .collect::<Vec<_>>()\n                .join(\"\\n\")\n        );\n    }\n\n    // Assert JSON output if expected_output.json exists.\n    let expected_output_path = fixture.join(\"expected_output.json\");\n    if expected_output_path.exists() && !stdout.is_empty() {\n        let expected_json: serde_json::Value =\n            serde_json::from_str(&fs::read_to_string(&expected_output_path).unwrap())\n                .expect(\"invalid expected_output.json\");\n        let actual_json = normalize_json(&stdout, work_dir);\n        assert_json_matches(&expected_json, &actual_json, \"$\");\n    }\n}\n\n// ── Auto-discovered fixture tests ────────────────────────────────────\n\n/// Run ALL fixture directories. Each is an independent test case.\n/// This function discovers fixtures at runtime, so adding a directory\n/// requires no code changes.\n#[test]\nfn fixture_tests() {\n    let fixtures = discover_fixtures();\n    assert!(\n        !fixtures.is_empty(),\n        \"no fixtures found in {}\",\n        fixtures_dir().display()\n    );\n\n    let mut failures = vec![];\n\n    for fixture result {\n            let msg = if let Some(s) = e.downcast_ref::<String>() {\n                s.clone()\n            } else if let Some(s) = e.downcast_ref::<&str>() {\n        \"{} of {} fixtures failed:\\n\\n{}\",\n            failures.len(),\n            fixtures.len(),\n            report\n        );\n    }\n}\n\n// ── Error fixtures: assert structured error error_fixtures_have_structured_fields() {\n    let error_fixtures: Vec<PathBuf> = discover_fixtures()\n        .into_iter()\n        .filter(|f| {\n            let name = error_op[\"what\"].is_string(),\n                \"fixture '{}': error missing 'what'\",\n                name\n            );\n            assert!(\n                error_op[\"where\"].is_string(),\n
